## Diagram 2

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Client
    participant LostException
    participant PackageContainerEventBusinessLogic
    participant BasePackageContainerException
    
    Client->>LostException: handleContainerException(container, container_business, exception, attributes)
    alt exception is None
        LostException->>Client: return (early exit)
    else exception exists
        LostException->>PackageContainerEventBusinessLogic: get_last_event(container)
        PackageContainerEventBusinessLogic-->>LostException: last_event
        LostException->>PackageContainerEventBusinessLogic: get_delivery_event(container)
        PackageContainerEventBusinessLogic-->>LostException: delivered_event
        LostException->>BasePackageContainerException: handle_eta_and_lcs_on_exception_change(container, last_event, delivered_event, exception)
        BasePackageContainerException-->>LostException: void
        LostException->>Client: void
    end
```


## Diagram 4

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> Initialized: __init__(reason_code)
    Initialized --> ProcessingMilestone: handleMilestoneEvent()
    Initialized --> ProcessingException: handleContainerException()
    ProcessingException --> CheckException: Check if exception exists
    CheckException --> EarlyReturn: exception is None
    CheckException --> FetchEvents: exception exists
    FetchEvents --> GetLastEvent: get_last_event()
    GetLastEvent --> GetDeliveryEvent: get_delivery_event()
    GetDeliveryEvent --> HandleETA: handle_eta_and_lcs_on_exception_change()
    HandleETA --> [*]
    EarlyReturn --> [*]
    ProcessingMilestone --> [*]
```
